         <script>
          /*** Client Side Metrics Code ***/
		P.when('jQuery', 'cf', 'ready').execute(function($) {
			var A9SL_callOnScroll = null;
			var appeared = false;
			var widgetId = "sponsoredLinks";
			var tableClass = "SponsoredLinkColumnAds";
			var viewSelector = ".SponsoredLinkColumnAds tr:first";
			var marketplace = "US";
			var requestTag = "ZWy8WPuaFmr71Vkj";
			var samplingType = "0";
			var sessionId = "181-6322926-2365634";
			var hoverTimeEnter = 0; // milliseconds
			var hoverTimeDef = 1000;  // milliseconds
			
			var fVip = "https://fls-na.amazon.com";
			var fApiVersion = "1";
			var fChannelId = "a9-sl";
			var fChannelVersion = "1";
			var fAction = "OP";
			var foresterUrlBase = [fVip, fApiVersion, fChannelId, fChannelVersion, fAction, "?"].join("/");
			
			function sendToForester(queryParams) {
				var repeatFlag = 0;
			
				// Back and forward button detection (if information is present)
				/*** NOTE: Disabled on Search pages! ***/
				/*
				var bfDetect;
		       	if (document.ue_backdetect &amp;&amp; document.ue_backdetect.ue_back) {
		         	bfDetect = document.ue_backdetect.ue_back;
		           	if (bfDetect.value &gt; 2) {
		            	repeatFlag = 1;
		           	}
		       	}
				*/
				
				if (repeatFlag === 0) {
					var queryString = "";
					for (key in queryParams) {
						queryString += key + "=" + encodeURIComponent(queryParams[key]) + "&amp;";
					}
					new Image().src = foresterUrlBase
										+ queryString
										+ "marketplace=" + encodeURIComponent(marketplace)
										+ "&amp;sessionId=" + encodeURIComponent(sessionId)
										+ "&amp;samplingType=" + encodeURIComponent(samplingType)
										+ "&amp;requestTag=" + encodeURIComponent(requestTag);
				}
			}

			function elementIsViewable (selector) {
				return ( elementHasHeightAndWidth(selector) &amp;&amp; isScrolledIntoView(selector) &amp;&amp; $(selector).is(":visible") );
			}

			function isScrolledIntoView(elem) {
			    var docViewTop = $(window).scrollTop();
			    var docViewBottom = docViewTop + $(window).height();

			    var elemTop = $(elem).offset().top;
			    var elemBottom = elemTop + $(elem).height();

			    return ((elemBottom &lt;= docViewBottom) &amp;&amp; (elemTop &gt;= docViewTop));
			}

			function elementHasHeightAndWidth (elem) {
				var height = $(elem).height();
				var width = $(elem).width();

				return (height &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; width &gt; 0);
			}
			//---GATHER PAGELOAD EVENT DATA---
			var pageLoadedParams = {};
			pageLoadedParams["eventType"] = "0";
			pageLoadedParams["reformatType"] = "0"; // forced parameter until we instrument this on search

			// Ad-blocking detection
			/*
				Note: The definition of visibility differs between jQuery 1.3.1 (and older) and jQuery 1.3.2+
			*/
			if ( $("#"+widgetId).is(':hidden') ||  !elementHasHeightAndWidth("#"+widgetId) ) {
				pageLoadedParams["adblockOn"] = "1";
			} else {
				pageLoadedParams["adblockOn"] = "0";
			}

			// check for appearance upon load even if no scrolling/resizing happens
			if ( appeared === false &amp;&amp; elementIsViewable(viewSelector) ) {
				appeared = true;
				pageLoadedParams["widgetInitView"] = "1";	
			} else {
				pageLoadedParams["widgetInitView"] = "0";
			}

			// Browser dimensions
			pageLoadedParams["browserDimX"] = $(window).width(); 
			pageLoadedParams["browserDimY"] = $(window).height();

			// Ads location
			pageLoadedParams["adsLocX"] = $("#"+widgetId).offset().left;
			pageLoadedParams["adsLocY"] = $("#"+widgetId).offset().top;

			// Screen resolution
			pageLoadedParams["screenResX"] = screen.width;
			pageLoadedParams["screenResY"] = screen.height;
			
			//Page Depth
			pageLoadedParams["pageDepth"] = $(document).height();

			//--- SEND PAGE LOAD EVENT DATA ---
			sendToForester(pageLoadedParams);
			

			//similar to callonvisible https://code.amazon.com/packages/P13NClientSideLogging/blobs/mainline/--/browser-scripts/source/callOnVisible/callOnVisible.js
			if (A9SL_callOnScroll === null){
				var lastCheck = 0; // timestamp to prevent us messing with the DOM too often
				var callCheckPending = false; // flag to prevent queueing up of multiple event handler calls
				A9SL_callOnScroll = function (){
					if (callCheckPending){
						return; // Haven't serviced last A9SL_callOnScrollIfNeeded call, yet
					}
					
					// Calculate the remaining time in the 200ms time interval 
					var diff = new Date().getTime() - lastCheck;
					var checkDelay = 0;
					if (diff &lt; 200){
						checkDelay = 200 - diff;
					} else checkDelay = 10;
					
					callCheckPending = true;
					
					
					// Call this function outside of the scroll handler (setTimeout) to avoid slowing down scrolling.
					var A9SL_callIfNeeded = function(){
					
						// check if the ad is seen
						if ((appeared === false) &amp;&amp; elementIsViewable(viewSelector) ){
							appeared = true;
							var params = {};
							params["eventType"] = "1";
							params["widgetScrollView"] = "1";
							
							sendToForester(params);
							$(window).unbind('scroll',A9SL_callOnScroll);
						}
						
						//Record the time it is checked
						callCheckPending = false;
						lastCheck = new Date().getTime();
					};
					setTimeout(A9SL_callIfNeeded, checkDelay);
				};
				
				$(window).bind('scroll', A9SL_callOnScroll);
			}
				
		
			// hover bind
			$("#"+widgetId).hover(
				function () {
					hoverTimeEnter = new Date().getTime();
				},
				function () {
					var hoverTimeExit = new Date().getTime();
					if ( (hoverTimeExit - hoverTimeEnter) &gt;= hoverTimeDef ){
						$("#"+widgetId).unbind("mouseenter mouseleave");

					 	var params = {};
						params["eventType"] = "2";
						params["hoverOnWidget"] = "1";

						sendToForester(params);
					}
				}
			);

		});
		

	P.when('jQuery','ready').execute(function($){
	    var jsonAds = '[{"redirectUrl":"http://rd.a9.com/srv/redirect/?info=AK0xAdbKX4A4feTdWzdtt3bHxQbWh40n-z0vC3xGLCJRkFTI40hizdRAcqM4Tj0fuUumpJF1yINK5PJmKNG9GNG5QS0aS4bN8yawQ5M-VCuhLborZfSU8DV6WV46CkqfKXQJfM56Uw9IxqOTNQGYf.pYAMGIu6PwqeSVNtZZuc4ASDOimwcEcLw.tzjwkCYw36v0Ipnp24HlDAqKVEyhK35K5.duNRLQqR--XM9DdXxrinUW84EP7GByezUsB4TMAyL-MutpIMb7GyZ8nC2KpI5BU-A6TL4eBZeTLVr802jMhK54DPdBqQMJUnBDeZO8egnDtPJVc.ye9BEUXC2UfdosHAbGekmZwEecaeCdTlAazaPjGW94UvLFZxVaUiyWrZyVrRI9qZgqPaVcCOFKrV4kNafRGmLKhUv7XbE7iQWcJjmjrhlzGfBmhC1paynnogr5jM1nrkZVXc1cO14VW7H5ZFHJUIKEZwPOiVVQQWswQrMMGY0FzgwhnB3bXUTiobb-3KAEV0w9NkAreG1wX69FPu4J8RKVNXiutiOZGLbzlvpG7fQNDgbsbZ0u9yKkWJVIy2bpnA7R5NpY2q7XmhVUKnVPxJb7fLKkin664Tz9-O5j7W-EXFy6r-LevGZauzoxUtxxg-Ko-9hqcRAcUS1CWsAKUYGHV.6Kc5yNxwFGHuhxMoN.r.xsouB.1xteish5uU2ukO8PejowhCHKur6RYd9oS5Ll9Um6XdVE2vaD&amp;awt=1&amp;s=","visibleUrl":"www.afcindustries.com/","description":"Standing &lt;b&gt;Desk&lt;/b&gt; 	    var feedbackFormAvailable = 0;
	    function showSLF() {
	         if(!feedbackFormAvailable) {
	           // Make a request to the handler with new ads 
	           $.post('/gp/product/aui_feedback_form_handler.html', { 'sid': '181-6322926-2365634','jsonAds' : escape(jsonAds) } ,function(data) {
	               $('#FeedbackFormDiv').html(data);
	               $('#FeedbackFormDiv').show();
	               $('#ShowFeedbackLinkDiv').hide();
	               $('#ResponseFeedbackLinkDiv').hide(); 
	               feedbackFormAvailable = 1;
	           });
	         } else {
	           $('#reports-ads-abuse-form').show();
	           $('#FeedbackFormDiv').show();
	           $('#reports-ads-abuse').show();
	           $('#ShowFeedbackLinkDiv').hide();
	           $('#ResponseFeedbackLinkDiv').hide(); 
	         }
	    }

	    $('#ShowFeedbackLinkDiv').css('opacity','1');
	    $('#ShowFeedbackLinkDiv').css('pointer-events','auto');

setTimeout(function () {
	P.when('jQuery', 'ready').execute(function($) {
		P.when('search-page-access').execute(function() {
			var successFlag = 0;
			SPUtils.afterEvent('spATFEvent', function () {
				if (!successFlag) {
					var browserWidth = $(window).width();
					var browserHeight = $(window).height();

						 { 'sessionCacheUpdateFlag' : '1',

         <script type="text/javascript">
          amzn.sx.utils.jsDepMgr.when('jQuery', 'deptRefinementCollapseExpand', function($) {
        
        function init(){
            setupView();
            addListeners();
        }

        function setupView(){
            $('#seeAllDepartmentClosed1').show();
            $('#fewDep').show();
            $('#seeAllDepartmentOpen1').hide();
        }

        function addListeners(){
            $showHideLinks.click( handleToggleLinkClick );
            $smartAPSSortUpdate.click( handleSmartAPSSortUpdate);
        }

        function handleToggleLinkClick( e ){
            var $el = $( e.currentTarget ),
                elToShow = $el.attr( "data-el-to-show"),
                elToHide = $el.attr( "data-el-to-hide");
            toggleElements( $( elToShow ),  $( elToHide ) );
            e.preventDefault();
            return false;
        }

        function handleSmartAPSSortUpdate(e){
            var dynamicID = $(e.currentTarget).attr("data-dynamic-id");
            smartAPSSortUpdate( dynamicID );
            e.preventDefault();
            return false;
        }

        function toggleElements( $toShow, $toHide ){
            $toHide.hide();
            $toShow.show();
        }

        
        var $showHideLinks = $(".s-hack-show-hide-el"),
            $smartAPSSortUpdate = $(".s-hack-smart-aps-sort-update");

        
        init();

    });
         </script>

    var cnt = 0;
    function executeApsDeepPaginationPleaseRefinePrompt() {
        var prompt, curSearch = location.hash || location.search || '';
        if (($.pageContext.baseRH !== (encodeURIComponent('i:aps,k:') + $.pageContext.searchKeywords)) ||
